### [192] [LLM as Clinical Graph Structure Refiner: Enhancing Representation Learning in EEG Seizure Diagnosis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28178)
*Lincan Li,Zheng Chen,Yushun Dong*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种利用大语言模型精炼EEG图边的两阶段图学习框架，以减少噪声导致的冗余或无关连接，从而提升自动癫痫检测性能与图结构可解释性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: EEG信号噪声强，传统相关性或学习式图构建方法容易产生冗余、无关边，削弱图表示质量并限制下游癫痫检测效果。作者受LLM推理与上下文理解能力启发，希望用其对图边进行语义与统计信息驱动的筛选。

Method: 框架分两阶段：首先验证LLM作为边精炼器可识别并移除冗余连接；随后构建完整方案，先用Transformer边预测器与多层感知机生成初始图并为候选边赋概率分数，经阈值筛选后，再由LLM基于节点对的文本特征和统计特征判断边是否保留。

Result: 在TUSZ数据集上的实验表明，LLM精炼后的图学习框架提升了癫痫检测任务性能，同时生成了更干净、更具可解释性的图结构。

Conclusion: LLM可作为有效的图边精炼模块，缓解EEG噪声引起的错误连接问题，改善图表示学习质量，并为医学EEG图建模提供一种兼具性能和解释性的方向。

Abstract: Electroencephalogram (EEG) signals are vital for automated seizure detection, but their inherent noise makes robust representation learning challenging. Existing graph construction methods, whether correlation-based or learning-based, often generate redundant or irrelevant edges due to the noisy nature of EEG data. This significantly impairs the quality of graph representation and limits downstream task performance. Motivated by the remarkable reasoning and contextual understanding capabilities of large language models (LLMs), we explore the idea of using LLMs as graph edge refiners. Specifically, we propose a two-stage framework: we first verify that LLM-based edge refinement can effectively identify and remove redundant connections, leading to significant improvements in seizure detection accuracy and more meaningful graph structures. Building on this insight, we further develop a robust solution where the initial graph is constructed using a Transformer-based edge predictor and multilayer perceptron, assigning probability scores to potential edges and applying a threshold to determine their existence. The LLM then acts as an edge set refiner, making informed decisions based on both textual and statistical features of node pairs to validate the remaining connections. Extensive experiments on TUSZ dataset demonstrate that our LLM-refined graph learning framework not only enhances task performance but also yields cleaner and more interpretable graph representations.

</details>

### [193] [On Coded Caching Systems with Decentralized Linear Coding Placement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27073)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 编码缓存可用用户端本地存储换取峰值时段通信负载降低；已有工作多关注集中式放置或去中心化非编码放置，而随机线性编码放置的基本性能极限尚不清楚。

Conclusion: 随机线性编码放置下的去中心化编码缓存具有可刻画的基本极限；在满足特定条件时，所提界给出了最坏情况负载的精确表征。

Abstract: Coded caching is a technique that leverages locally cached contents at the end users to reduce the network's peak-time communication load. Coded caching has been shown to achieve significant performance gains with a centralized placement orchestrated by the server and is thus considered a promising technique to boost performance in future networks by effectively trading off bandwidth for storage. To tackle issues caused by the synchronized placement, previous works focused on decentralized placement and found the exact worst-case load with uncoded placement. In this paper, we focus on a decentralized coded caching system with random linear coding placement, and investigate the fundamental limits of a linear coding placement where each user independently and uniformly caches random linear coding symbols of a single file. We propose achievable and converse bounds on the worst-case load, which are shown to meet under certain conditions.

### [194] [Low-Complexity Run-Length-Limited ISI-Mitigation (RLIM) Codes for Molecular Communication](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27104)
*Melih Şahin,Ozgur B. Akan*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文提出一种用于分子通信RLIM码的枚举式实现，避免完整码本存储，将存储复杂度由指数级降至多项式级，并支持更大维度下获得更好的误码率表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分子通信存在严重符号间干扰，因此需要约束编码降低ISI。已有游程长度受限的ISI缓解码具有良好误码率性能，但原始实现依赖完整码本生成与存储，存储随维度指数增长，不适合存储和计算能力受限的纳米级分子通信节点，也限制了更大信息维度的探索。

Method: 论文用基于Cover排序框架的枚举式编码/解码替代完整码本存储，结合恒重游程长度受限序列计数和累积重量层偏移。该方法保留原RLIM码本选择机制和基于投影的译码行为，仅需存储多项式规模的计数表。

Result: 存储与运行时间测量表明，该实现将原先的指数级存储需求降为多项式级。扩散型分子通信仿真显示，由于可访问更大维度的RLIM码，在测试设置中可提升最佳可达误码率性能。

Conclusion: 该工作解决了RLIM码在分子通信中由码本存储引起的实现瓶颈，使其更适合资源受限场景，并为探索大维度、低ISI、高可靠性的分子通信编码方案提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Molecular communication suffers from severe inter-symbol interference, which makes constrained coding essential for reliable transmission. Run-length-limited ISI-mitigation codes are attractive because they select low-weight constrained codebooks, reducing ISI while allowing more molecules to be assigned to each transmitted 1-symbol under the usual molecular-communication normalization. Previous results showed strong bit-error-rate performance for these codes, but their original realization required full codebook generation and storage. This exponential storage growth is unsuitable for resource-constrained molecular communication channels and also limits the exploration of larger information dimensions. This is particularly important for nano-scale molecular communication, where transmitter and receiver nodes are expected to operate under severe memory and computational constraints. This paper removes that realization bottleneck by replacing full codebook storage with an enumerative realization based on Cover's ranking framework, constant-weight run-length-limited counting, and cumulative weight-layer offsets. The resulting encoder and decoder preserve the selected RLIM codebooks and the original projection-based decoding behavior while storing only polynomial-size counting tables. Storage and runtime measurements confirm the resulting exponential-to-polynomial reduction, and diffusion-based molecular-communication simulations show that the newly accessible larger-dimensional RLIM regimes can improve the best attainable bit-error-rate performance in the tested settings.

</details>


### [195] [Harnessing the Freedom of Non-Uniformity in Monostatic ISAC with Antenna Flexibility](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27571)
*Zhe Wang,Mahmoud Zaher,Vitaly Petrov,Emil Björnson*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文研究单站ISAC系统中的灵活非均匀阵列设计，通过动态分配候选天线的发射、接收或 inactive 模式，并联合优化波束成形与天线模式，以提升通信和感知协同性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统均匀阵列往往依赖增加激活天线数量来提升性能，硬件成本和功耗较高；在ISAC系统中，如何利用天线几何结构与模式选择实现更高效的通信速率与感知约束满足，是本文的核心动机。

Method: 作者构建了以通信和速率最大化为目标的联合优化问题，同时考虑ISAC波束成形、天线模式分配、感知约束、功率约束和天线模式约束。求解上采用交替优化框架，并结合加权最小均方误差、连续松弛惩罚方法和逐次凸近似。

Result: 数值结果表明，所提出的非均匀阵列相比均匀阵列基线可获得更高的通信和速率，尤其在激活天线数量较少时增益更明显；同时，它能用显著更少的激活天线达到甚至超过均匀阵列基线性能。

Conclusion: 几何感知的非均匀阵列设计是比单纯增加天线规模更具效率和潜力的ISAC阵列设计方案，可在较低硬件激活成本下实现优越的通信性能并满足感知需求。

Abstract: This paper studies flexible non-uniform array design for monostatic integrated sensing and communication (ISAC) systems. An antenna pool is considered at the base station, where each candidate antenna can be dynamically assigned to transmit, receive, or inactive modes, such that a non-uniform effective array is jointly constructed with the ISAC precoding design. We formulate a sum communication rate maximization problem by jointly optimizing the ISAC beamforming schemes and antenna-mode assignment under sensing, power, and antenna mode constraints. We develop an alternating-optimization-based solution framework mainly with the aid of weighted minimum mean square error, continuous relaxation-based penalty, and successive convex approximation. Numerical results show that the proposed non-uniform array achieves higher sum-rates than the uniform-array baselines, with particularly large gains when the number of activated antennas is small. Moreover, the proposed non-uniform array can achieve, and in some cases exceed, the performance of uniform array baselines with substantially fewer activated antennas, highlighting geometry-aware non-uniform array design as a compelling alternative to brute-force antenna scaling-based array design.

</details>


### [196] [Why Self-Supervised Encoders Want to Be Normal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.27743)
*Yuval Domb*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文提出一个基于信息瓶颈原则的编码器-解码器学习框架，将表示学习解释为以 KL 散度为失真的率失真问题，并用 SIGReg 作为高斯松弛的分布正则化方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有编码器-解码器与信息瓶颈方法在几何解释、先验分布到欧氏正则化的联系、以及弱监督/自监督场景下的可估计训练目标方面仍不够统一；作者希望建立一个同时具有信息论、几何和可实现损失函数解释的框架。

Method: 作者将信息瓶颈重写为 KL 失真的率失真问题，分析预测流形在概率单纯形中的软聚类结构；推导从平坦 Dirichlet 先验到指数族再到各向同性高斯的变换链，并量化熵开销；基于 Conditional Entropy Bottleneck 分解构造监督、半监督和自监督损失，其中半监督和自监督使用 SIGReg 分布正则化，监督/半监督损失通过 minibatch 边缘分布估计而不依赖变分界。

Result: 在玩具数据和 FashionMNIST 上，实验验证了理论预测的率失真权衡，并显示非参数估计器与标准变分方法相比具有竞争力。

Conclusion: 该工作给出了信息瓶颈编码器-解码器学习的统一几何与信息论解释，说明 SIGReg 可视为最大熵单纯形先验到高斯空间的松弛实现，并可作为有限监督或无监督场景下的原则性分布正则化工具。

Abstract: We develop a geometric and information-theoretic framework for encoder-decoder learning built on the Information Bottleneck (IB) principle. Recasting IB as a rate-distortion problem with Kullback-Leibler (KL) divergence as distortion, we show that the optimal representation at any distortion level is a soft clustering of the \emph{predictive manifold} $\mathcal{M}=\{p(Y|x):x\in\mathcal{X}\}$ inside the probability simplex, admitting a linear decoder in the canonical parameterization.
  We derive a chain of exact transformations, from flat Dirichlet to exponential to isotropic Gaussian, connecting the maximum entropy prior on the simplex to Euclidean space, with quantified entropy overhead at each step, and show that Sketched Isotropic Gaussian Regularization (SIGReg) implements a Gaussian relaxation of this principle whose overhead affects rate accounting but not achievable prediction. This relaxation provides a principled distributional regularizer for learning with limited or no supervision.
  Using the Conditional Entropy Bottleneck (CEB) decomposition, we derive concrete encoder losses for supervised and semi-supervised settings, estimated via minibatch marginals without variational bounds. In the self-supervised setting, the CEB conditional rate is replaced by a view-prediction proxy. SIGReg serves as the distributional regularizer for both the semi-supervised and self-supervised settings.
  Experiments on toy problems and FashionMNIST confirm the predicted rate-distortion trade-offs and show that the non-parametric estimator is competitive with the standard variational approach.

</details>


### [197] [Perfectly Private Over-the-Air Computation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.28080)
*Shudi Weng,Ming Xiao,Mikael Skoglund*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文探讨如何在空中计算（AirComp）中同时实现完美隐私与准确聚合，结论是二者并不天然冲突。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AirComp 中存在隐私与可计算性的两难：实数域运算有利于可逆和精确计算，但会引入统计相关性导致隐私泄露；模运算可削弱输出与原始消息的相关性，却在非素数群或实数域场景下面临可逆性不适定问题。因此，论文试图回答完美隐私是否与 AirComp 本质冲突这一基础问题。

Method: 论文通过结合实数域运算与模运算的优势，设计一种利用二者相互作用的私有聚合机制，使计算过程既保持可恢复/可计算性，又使聚合输出与个体原始信息解耦，从而实现完美隐私。

Result: 研究表明，在适当设计下，AirComp 可以同时达到完美隐私和准确计算，支持 perfectly private aggregation。

Conclusion: 完美隐私并不必然与 AirComp 冲突；通过精心融合实数域与模运算，可以突破传统可逆性与去相关性之间的矛盾，实现隐私保护的精确空中聚合。

Abstract: This paper studies a key research question: how to achieve perfect privacy in over-the-air computation (AirComp)? The problem is particularly intriguing due to a dilemma. Real-field operations can ensure invertibility but generally introduce statistical dependence, resulting in inevitable privacy leakage. In contrast, modulo operations can decorrelate the output from the original message, but suffer from the ill-posed invertibility when applied over non-prime groups (e.g., the real field). This raises a subtle yet fundamental question: Does perfect privacy intrinsically conflict with AirComp? We show that the answer is no. By carefully leveraging the interplay between real-field and modulo operations, perfect privacy and accurate computation can, in fact, be achieved simultaneously, enabling perfectly private aggregation.

</details>
